Trigger InEnemyLandsTrigger1
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition InEnemyLands 
       and Attribute Command >= 4
       and not Trait InEnemyRegion > 2

 Affects InEnemyRegion 1 Chance 50
 
;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition InEnemyLands 
       and Attribute Command < 4
       and not Trait InEnemyRegion > 2

 Affects InEnemyRegion 1 Chance 100

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition InEnemyLands 
       and Trait InFriendlyRegion > 0

 Affects InEnemyRegion 2 Chance 100

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition not InEnemyLands
       and Attribute Command >= 4
       and not Trait InFriendlyRegion > 2

 Affects InFriendlyRegion 1 Chance 100

       and Attribute Command < 4
       and not Trait InFriendlyRegion > 2

;********* BLOODLINES TRIGGERS - ROYAL HOUSES *********
;------------------------------------------
Trigger Rebel_Found_RoyalHouse
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

 Condition FactionType slave
       and I_TurnNumber = 0 

 Affects HouseMember 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger FoundRoyalHouse 
 WhenToTest BecomesFactionLeader

 Condition Trait BiologicalSon = 1
       and Trait HouseMember = 0
       and Trait Factionleader > 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_English = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_French = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_HRE = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Spanish = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Sicilian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Venetian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Milanese = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Pisan = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Scottish = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Greek = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Russian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Moorish = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Turkish = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Rum_Turkish = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Egyptian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Danish = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Portuguese = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Polish = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Hungarian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Serbian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Aragonese = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Lithuanian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Georgian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Norwegian = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Kievan = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Cumans = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Kwarezm = 0
       and Trait Royal_Blood_Jerusalem = 0

 Affects HouseFounder 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger SonofHouseFounder
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition FatherTrait HouseFounder > 0

 Affects HouseMember 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger SonofHouseMember
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition FatherTrait HouseMember > 0

 Affects HouseMember 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger DaughterofHouseFounder
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition FatherTrait HouseFounder > 0
       and AgentType = princess

 Affects HousePrincess 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger DaughterofHouseMember
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition FatherTrait HouseMember > 0
       and AgentType = princess

 Affects HousePrincess 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger SonofNewRoyalHouseFounder
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition FatherTrait HouseFounder > 0
       and Trait HouseMember = 0
       and Trait BiologicalSon > 0

 Affects HouseMember 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger BastardSonofNewRoyalHouseFounder
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition FatherTrait HouseFounder > 0
       and Trait HouseMember = 0
       and Trait BastardSon > 0

 Affects HouseMember 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger DaughterofNewHouseFounder
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition FatherTrait HouseFounder > 0
       and AgentType = princess
       and Trait HousePrincess = 0

 Affects HousePrincess 1 Chance 100

;********* MARRIAGE TRAIT TRIGGERS *********
;------------------------------------------
Trigger AI_marries
 WhenToTest CharacterMarries

 Condition FactionIsLocal

 Affects MarriageCertificate 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger family_generalmarries_daughterofkingprince
 WhenToTest CharacterMarriesPrincess

 Condition SpouseTrait DaughterofKingPrince > 0

 Affects WifeIsDaughterofKingPrince 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger family_general_marries_muslim1
 WhenToTest CharacterMarriesPrincess

 Condition not CharacterReligion islam
	   and SpouseAttribute Charm >= 6
       and SpouseTrait Princess_Royal_Blood_Moorish = 1
       and SpouseTrait Princess_Orthodox = 0
       and SpouseTrait Princess_Catholic = 0
       and SpouseTrait Princess_Pagan = 0
       and Attribute Piety <= 5 
       and Trait PublicAtheism <= 1
	   and Trait Muslim = 0
	   
 Affects Muslim 1 Chance 100
 Affects Orthodox -1 Chance 100
 Affects Pagan -1 Chance 100
 Affects Catholic -1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger family_general_marries_muslim12
 WhenToTest CharacterMarriesPrincess

 Condition not CharacterReligion islam
	   and SpouseTrait Princess_Royal_Blood_Moorish = 1
	   and SpouseAttribute Charm >= 6
	   and SpouseTrait Princess_Orthodox = 0
       and SpouseTrait Princess_Catholic = 0
       and SpouseTrait Princess_Pagan = 0
       
 Affects WifeIsMuslim 1 Chance 100
 
;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterMarriesPrincess

 Condition not CharacterReligion islam
	   and Trait Muslim = 0
	   and SpouseTrait Princess_Royal_Blood_Moorish = 1
	   and SpouseAttribute Charm < 6
       
 Affects WifeHasConverted 1 Chance 100

;*********************Pnut's Diseases - Pneumonia
;------------------------------------------

       and IsFactionLeader
       and Treasury < 0
       and SettlementsTaken >= 5
       and Attribute Authority <= 5
       and FactionIsLocal

       and CharacterReligion catholic

       and FactionIsLocal

 Condition IsRegionOneOf 199 Mecca_Province
       and AgentType = priest
       and CharacterReligion islam
       and TimeInRegion > 1
       and Trait PriestIslamicDoctrine = 0

 Affects PriestIslamicDoctrine 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger Priest_Visit_JerusalemRegion_All
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition IsRegionOneOf 190 Jerusalem_Province
       and AgentType = priest
       and not CharacterReligion pagan
       and TimeInRegion > 1
       and Trait StrongFaith <= 4

 Affects StrongFaith 1 Chance 33

;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition IsRegionOneOf 190 Jerusalem_Province
       and AgentType = priest
       and CharacterReligion catholic
       and not FactionIsLocal
       and TimeInRegion > 1
       and Trait StrongFaith <= 4

 Affects StrongFaith 1 Chance 50

;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

       and FactionType cumans

 Affects StrongFaith 1 Chance 40

       and FatherTrait Disobedient >= 1
       and not Trait Badblood > 0
       and not Trait Disobedient >= 1 ;if already a traitor what is the point?

 Affects Badblood 1 Chance 100

;*********** EDUCATION TRIGGERS ***********
;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Start_edu_count
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition IsGeneral

 Affects Wantschool 16 Chance 100

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Military_birth_nonpagan
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition IsGeneral
       and not FactionType cumans
       and not FactionType lithuania 
       
 Affects MilitaryInclination 1 Chance 40

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Military_birth_cuman
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition IsGeneral
       and FactionType cumans

 Affects MilitaryInclination 1 Chance 70

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Military_birth_lithuania
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition IsGeneral
       and FactionType lithuania 

 Affects MilitaryInclination 1 Chance 70

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Governor_birth
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition IsGeneral
       and not Trait MilitaryInclination = 1

 Affects GovernorInclination 1 Chance 100

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Edu_timer
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

 Condition Trait Wantschool > 0
       and IsGeneral

 Affects Wantschool -1 Chance 100

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Scholar_birth
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition IsGeneral

 Affects WantsHigherEd 1 Chance 5

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Scholar_birth_father
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition IsGeneral
       and FatherTrait WantsHigherEd = 1 

 Affects WantsHigherEd 1 Chance 10

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Scholar_birth_intelligent
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge

 Condition IsGeneral
       and Trait Intelligent >= 1

 Affects WantsHigherEd 1 Chance 5

;--------------------------------------------
Trigger Inspiring_teacher
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition IsGeneral
       and HasAncType GreatAcademic

;********* ENVIOUSOFHEIR TRIGGERS *********
;------------------------------------------
Trigger SonofKing_EnviesHeir
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition FatherTrait Factionleader = 3
       and not IsFactionHeir
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and Attribute Loyalty <= 4
       and Trait EnviousOfHeir = 0

 Affects EnviousOfHeir 1 Chance 10

;------------------------------------------
Trigger SonofRegent_EnviesHeir
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition FatherTrait FactionRegent = 2
       and not IsFactionHeir
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and Attribute Loyalty <= 4
       and Trait EnviousOfHeir = 0

 Affects EnviousOfHeir 1 Chance 10

;------------------------------------------
Trigger EnviesHeir_NoMore
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition Trait EnviousOfHeir = 1
       and Attribute Loyalty >= 5

 Affects EnviousOfHeir -1 Chance 33

;------------------------------------------
Trigger EnviesHeir_IsHeir
 WhenToTest BecomesFactionHeir

 Condition Trait EnviousOfHeir > 0

 Affects EnviousOfHeir -1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger EnviesHeir_IsLeader
 WhenToTest BecomesFactionLeader

 Condition Trait EnviousOfHeir > 0

 Affects EnviousOfHeir -1 Chance 100

;********* EXCOMMUNICATION TRIGGERS ********* 
;------------------------------------------
Trigger ExcommunicatedProof 
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd 

 Condition IsFactionLeader
       and FactionExcommunicated
       and not Trait Excommunication >= 1
       and not Trait ExcommunicationJoke >= 1 

 Affects Excommunication 1 Chance 100
 Affects ExcommunicationJoke 2 Chance 33

;------------------------------------------
Trigger ReconciledProof
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition IsFactionLeader
       and not FactionExcommunicated
       and Trait Excommunication = 1 

 Affects Reconciliation 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger ReconciledtheJokerProof
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition IsFactionLeader
       and not FactionExcommunicated
       and Trait ExcommunicationJoke = 1 

 Affects Reconciliation 1 Chance 100

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

       and SettlementName Jerusalem
       and IsGeneral
       and CharacterReligion catholic
       and not Trait Visit_Jerusalem >= 1
       and not Trait Visit_Jerusalem2 >= 1
 
 Affects Visit_Jerusalem 1 Chance 50

       and not Trait RivalConquer_Constantinople >= 1
       and not Trait GreekConquer_Constantinople >= 1
       and not Trait RivalConquer_Constantinople1 >= 1
       and not Trait GreekConquer_Constantinople1 >= 1

 Affects RivalConquer_Constantinople 1 Chance 100
 Affects GreekConquer_Constantinople 1 Chance 100

       and not Trait RivalConquer_Constantinople1 >= 1
       and not Trait GreekConquer_Constantinople1 >= 1

 Affects RivalConquer_Constantinople1 2 Chance 10
 Affects GreekConquer_Constantinople1 2 Chance 10

Trigger VendettaAgainstVenice
 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition IsGeneral
       and not WonBattle
       and BattleSuccess > average
       and I_ConflictType Normal
       and BattleOdds >= 0.5
       and GeneralFoughtFaction venice
       and Trait VendettaSet = 0

 Affects VendettaVenice 1 Chance 50

       and not WonBattle
       and BattleSuccess > clear

       and RandomPercent > 44
       and RandomPercent < 51

       and NumCapturedSoldiers > 200

 Affects BattleChivalry 1 Chance 50

 Condition RansomType release
       and NumCapturedSoldiers > 400

 Affects BattleChivalry 1 Chance 75

       and NumCapturedSoldiers > 200

;------------------------------------------
;VictorVirtue   Thresholds 10, 20, 30
;if this is to fast edit   Thresholds
Trigger triumphs_in_battle_standard
 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition IsGeneral
       and WonBattle
       and BattleSuccess < clear
       and BattleOdds < 2.5
       and NumFriendsInBattle > 750 

 Affects VictorVirtue 1 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger triumphs_in_battle_clear
 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition IsGeneral
       and WonBattle
       and BattleSuccess = clear
       and BattleOdds < 2.5
       and NumFriendsInBattle > 750 

 Affects VictorVirtue 2 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger triumphs_in_battle_crushing
 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition IsGeneral
       and WonBattle
       and BattleSuccess > clear
       and BattleOdds < 2.5
       and NumFriendsInBattle > 750 

 Affects VictorVirtue 3 Chance 100

;------------------------------------------
Trigger triumphs_in_siege
 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition IsGeneral
       and WonBattle
       and BattleSuccess >= clear
       and I_ConflictType Siege
       and GeneralNumKillsInBattle > 6
       and BattleOdds <= 0.9
       and NumFriendsInBattle > 500 

 Affects VictorVirtue 1 Chance 100
 Affects VictorVirtue 1 Chance 40

 Affects VictorVirtue 1 Chance 100

 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition IsGeneral
       and not WonBattle
       and PercentageRoutedOffField >= 40
       and FactionIsLocal

 Affects BadDisciplinarian 1 Chance 25

 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition WonBattle
       and IsGeneral
       and BattleOdds < 0.6
       and PercentageRoutedOffField < 25

 Affects Disciplinarian 1 Chance 20

       and not Trait BattleChivalry >= 1
       and not Trait BattleDread >= 1
       and IsGeneral

 Affects Brave 1 Chance 15 
 Affects Bloodthirsty 1 Chance 10

 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition GeneralNumKillsInBattle > 10
       and not Trait BattleChivalry > 0
       and IsGeneral

 Affects BattleDread 1 Chance 8 
 Affects Brave 1 Chance 15 
 Affects Bloodthirsty 1 Chance 10

       and not Trait BattleDread > 0
       and IsGeneral

 Affects BattleChivalry 1 Chance 8

 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition not WasAttacker
       and WonBattle
       and IsGeneral
       and BattleOdds <= 0.5
       and GeneralFoughtInCombat
       and not Trait BattleDread > 0
       and NumFriendsInBattle > 500

 Affects BattleChivalry 1 Chance 75

 WhenToTest PostBattle

       and WonBattle
       and IsGeneral
       and BattleOdds <= 0.5
       and GeneralFoughtInCombat
       and Trait BattleDread > 0
       and NumFriendsInBattle > 350

 Affects BattleDread 1 Chance 75

Trigger battle_BattleChivalry_SpareRouters
 WhenToTest PostBattle

 Condition WonBattle
       and PercentageEnemyKilled < 80
       and GeneralFoughtInCombat
       and IsGeneral

       and NumFriendsInBattle > 500
       and FactionIsLocal

 Affects BattleChivalry 1 Chance 30

       and DistanceCapital <= 50

       and DistanceCapital <= 50
       and I_EventCounter great_fair_false > 0

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition CharacterIsLocal
       and AgentType = priest
       and DistanceCapital <= 60
       and I_EventCounter great_council_true > 0

 Affects Dogmatic 1 Chance 100
 Affects StrongFaith 1 Chance 25

;------------ Troubadours ------------------
Trigger troubadours_accepted_leader
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

 Condition CharacterIsLocal
       and IsFactionLeader
       and I_EventCounter troubadours_event_true > 0

 Affects StrategyChivalry 1 Chance 10
 Affects Poet 1 Chance 25
 Affects Cultured 1 Chance 25

 Condition CharacterIsLocal
       and AgentType = princess
       and DistanceCapital <= 50
       and I_EventCounter troubadours_event_true > 0

 Affects FairWoman 1 Chance 50

;--- spawn_character trait boost ----------
Trigger spawn_char_trait_boost_priest_pagan
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

 Condition AgentType = priest
       and Trait NaturalPriestSkill = 0 
       and CharacterReligion pagan

 Affects NaturalPriestSkill 1 Chance 100
 Affects NaturalPriestSkill 1 Chance 70
 Affects NaturalPriestSkill 1 Chance 20
 Affects Warmonger 1 Chance 40
 Affects Warmonger 1 Chance 25
 Affects StrongFaith 1 Chance 65
 Affects StrongFaith 1 Chance 55
 Affects DivineProtectionPagan 1 Chance 45
 Affects HeresyImmunityAI 1 Chance 80
 
;------------------------------------------

 Condition AgentType = priest
       and Trait NaturalPriestSkill = 0 
       and not CharacterReligion pagan

 Affects NaturalPriestSkill 1 Chance 100
 Affects NaturalPriestSkill 1 Chance 70
 Affects NaturalPriestSkill 1 Chance 20
 Affects Peaceful 1 Chance 50
 Affects Peaceful 1 Chance 35
 Affects StrongFaith 1 Chance 65
 Affects Dogmatic 1 Chance 85
 Affects DivineProtection 1 Chance 45
 Affects HeresyImmunityAI 1 Chance 80

; BYZANTINE CAREER TRIGGERS

Trigger Career_start
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

Condition not EndedInSettlement
and IsGeneral
and FactionType byzantium
and not IsFactionLeader
and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 0

Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 8
;----------------------------------------------------

Trigger Comes_to_Hiliarches
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

Condition not EndedInSettlement
       and IsGeneral
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 1


Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------

Trigger Hiliarches_to_Taxiarches
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

Condition not EndedInSettlement
       and IsGeneral
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 2


Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------

Trigger Taxiarches_to_Droungarios
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

Condition not EndedInSettlement
       and IsGeneral
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 3
 

Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------

Trigger Droungarios_to_Merarches
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

Condition not EndedInSettlement
       and IsGeneral
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 4
       and Trait GoodCommander >= 1

Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------
Trigger Merarches_to_Tourmarches
WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

Condition IsGeneral
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 5
       and Trait GoodCommander >= 2

Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------
Trigger Tourmarches_to_Strategos
WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

Condition IsGeneral
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 6
       and Trait GoodCommander >= 3


Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------
Trigger Strategos_to_Sevastos
WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

Condition IsGeneral
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 7
       and Trait GoodCommander >= 4
 

Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------
Trigger Sevastos_to_Magistrus
WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

Condition IsGeneral
       and not IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium = 8
       and Trait GoodCommander >= 5
 

Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium 1 Chance 100

Trigger Heir_Become_Emperor_Remove_Rank
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

 Condition IsFactionLeader
       and FactionType byzantium
       and AgentType = family
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium <= 8
       and Trait Military_Career_In_Byzantium > 0
 
 
Affects Military_Career_In_Byzantium -68 Chance 100

Trigger TooOldSickly
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd
 
Condition IsGeneral
       and CharacterAge > 61
       and Trait Sickly > 0
       and Trait TooOldToFight = 0
 
Affects TooOldToFight 1 Chance 25

;------------------------------------------
Trigger TooOldNormal
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd
 
Condition IsGeneral
       and CharacterAge > 61
       and Trait Sickly < 1
       and Trait Robust < 1
       and Trait TooOldToFight = 0
 
Affects TooOldToFight 1 Chance 15

;------------------------------------------
Trigger TooOldRobust
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd
 
Condition IsGeneral
       and CharacterAge > 61
       and Trait Robust > 0
       and Trait TooOldToFight = 0
 
Affects TooOldToFight 1 Chance 7

;------------------------------------------
Trigger Alzheimer
WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd
 
Condition IsGeneral
       and CharacterAge > 65
 
Affects Senile 1 Chance 2

WhenToTest CeasedFactionLeader 
 
Condition Trait Factionleader = 3 
                                                                 
Affects Factionleader -2 Chance 100

Condition Trait Factionleader = 2

 WhenToTest OfferedForAdoption

 Condition I_EventCounter fatimid_evolution = 1
    and FactionType egypt

 Affects Royal_Blood_Mamluk 1 Chance 33

 WhenToTest OfferedForAdoption

 Condition I_EventCounter zengid_evolution = 1
    and FactionType kwarezm

 Affects Royal_Blood_Mamluk 1 Chance 33
